a Form&#160;6-K if submitted to furnish a report or other document that the

rules of the home country exchange on which the registrant&#8217;s securities 
are traded, as long as the report or other document is not a press release, is 
not required to be and has not been distributed to the registrant&#8217;s 
security holders, and, if discussing a material event, has already been the 
subject of a Form&#160;6-K submission or other Commission filing on

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">Pursuant to section 11.3 of NI 51-102, 
this report briefly describes the matters voted upon and the outcome of the
votes at the annual general meeting of the shareholders of Entr&#233;e Gold Inc.
held on June 27, 2013 in Vancouver, British Columbia.</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;

</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;registered address&#8221; of a shareholder means the 
address of the shareholder recorded in the central securities register of the 
Company;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(h)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;registered owner&#8221; or &#8220;registered 
holder&#8221; or &#8220;holder&#8221; when used with respect to a share of the 
Company means the person registered in the central securities register of the 
Company in respect of such share;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;regulations&#8221; means the regulations from time to 
time in force and made pursuant to the Business Corporations Act; 
and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(j)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;seal&#8221; means the common seal of the Company, if 
any.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">1.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Expressions referring to 
writing shall be construed as including printing, lithography, typewriting, 
photography, photocopying, facsimile transmission, electronic media and all 
other modes of representing or reproducing words in a visible form.</font></div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">1.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Words importing the 
singular include the plural and <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: 
inline">vice versa</font> and words importing a male person include a female 
person and a corporation.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">1.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font 
id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;</font></font></font></font></font>The definitions in the Business 
Corporations Act and the definitions and rules of construction in the <font 
style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Interpretation Act</font> (British 
Columbia) shall, with the necessary changes, so far as applicable, and unless 
the context requires otherwise, apply to these Articles.&#160;&#160;If there is 
a conflict between a definition in the Business Corporations Act and a 
definition or rule in the <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: 
inline">Interpretation Act </font>(British Columbia), the definition in the 
Business Corporations Act shall prevail.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">1.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The provisions contained 
in Table 1 to the Business Corporations Regulation shall not apply to the 
Company.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 2</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">SHARES AND SHARE 
CERTIFICATES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The authorized share 
structure of the Company shall consist of shares of a class or classes, which 
may be divided into one or more series, as described in the Notice of Articles 
of the Company.&#160;&#160;Each class of issued shares shall be evidenced by a 
distinct form of certificate.&#160;&#160;Every share certificate issued by the 
Company shall be in such form as the Directors may approve from time to time and
shall comply with, and be signed as required by, the Business Corporations 
Act.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2"
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Every shareholder is 
entitled, without charge, to (a) one certificate representing the share or 
shares of each class held by him; or (b) a non-transferable written 
acknowledgement of the shareholder&#8217;s right to obtain such a certificate, 
provided that in respect of a share or shares held jointly by several 
shareholders, the Company shall not be bound to issue more than one certificate,
and delivery of a certificate for a share to one of several joint registered 
holders or to his duly authorized agent shall be sufficient delivery to 
all.&#160;&#160;The Company shall not be bound to issue certificates 
representing redeemable shares if such shares are to be redeemed within one 
month of the date on which they were allotted.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Any share certificate or 
non-transferable written acknowledgment of a shareholder&#8217;s right to obtain
a share certificate may be sent to the shareholder by mail at the 
shareholder&#8217;s registered address and neither the Company nor any transfer 
agent shall be liable for any loss occasioned to the shareholder resulting from 
the loss or theft of any such share certificate or acknowledgement so 
sent.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>If a share certificate or 
a non-transferable written acknowledgment of the shareholder&#8217;s right to 
obtain a share certificate:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">is worn out or defaced, the Directors may, upon production to 
the Company of the certificate or the acknowledgment and upon such other terms, 
if any, as they may think fit, order the certificate or acknowledgment to be 
cancelled and issue a new certificate or acknowledgment in lieu thereof;
or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div align="center">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" 
width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
</table>
</div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">- 2 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div><br>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">is lost, stolen or destroyed, the Directors may, upon proof 
thereof to their satisfaction and upon such indemnity, if any, being given as 
they consider adequate, issue a new share certificate or acknowledgment in lieu 
thereof to the person entitled to such lost, stolen or destroyed certificate or 
acknowledgment.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div align="center">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" 
width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
</table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">2.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>If a share certificate 
represents more than one share and the registered owner thereof surrenders it to
the Company with a written request that the Company issue in his name two or 
more certificates each representing a specified number of shares and in the 
aggregate representing the same number of shares as the certificate so 
surrendered, the Directors shall cancel the certificate so surrendered and issue
in lieu thereof certificates in accordance with such request.</font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.6<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>If a shareholder owns 
shares of a class or series represented by more than one share certificate and 
surrenders the certificates to the Company with a written request that the 
Company issue in his name one certificate representing in the aggregate the same
number of shares as the certificates so surrendered, the Directors shall cancel 
the certificates so surrendered and issue in lieu thereof a certificate in 
accordance with such request.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.7<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The Directors may from 
time to time determine the amount of a charge, not exceeding an amount 
prescribed by the Business Corporations Act or the regulations, to be imposed 
for each certificate issued pursuant to Articles 2.4, 2.5 and 2.6.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2.8<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Except as required by law,
statute or these Articles, no person shall be recognized by the Company as 
holding any share upon any trust, and the Company shall not be bound by or 
compelled in any way to recognize (even when having notice thereof) any 
equitable, contingent, future or partial interest in any share or in any 
fractional part of a share or (except as provided by law, statute or these 
Articles or as ordered by a court of competent jurisdiction) any other rights in
respect of any share except an absolute right to the entirety thereof in its 
registered holder.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 3</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">ISSUE OF SHARES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">3.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>Subject to the Business Corporations Act and the rights 
of the holders of issued shares of the Company, the shares of the Company shall 
be under the control of the Directors, who may issue, allot, sell or otherwise 
dispose of the unissued shares, and issued shares held by the Company, at the 
times, to the persons, including Directors, in the manner, on the terms and 
conditions and for the issue prices (including any premium at which shares with 
par value may be issued) that the Directors may determine.&#160;&#160;The issue 
price for a share with par value must be equal to or greater than the par value 
of the share.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">3.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The Company may at any time, pay a reasonable commission
or allow a reasonable discount to any person in consideration of his subscribing
or agreeing to subscribe, whether absolutely or conditionally, for shares of the
Company, or procuring or agreeing to procure subscriptions, whether absolutely 
or conditionally, for any such shares.&#160;&#160;The Directors shall determine,
in their sole discretion, what is reasonable in the circumstances.</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div>&#160;
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;3 -</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">3.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The Company may pay such 
brokerage fee or other consideration as may be lawful for or in connection with 
the sale or placement of its securities.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">3.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Except as provided for by 
the Business Corporations Act, no share may be issued until it is fully paid and
the Company shall have received the full consideration therefor in cash, 
property or past services actually performed for the Company.&#160;&#160;A 
document evidencing indebtedness of the allottee is not property for the purpose
of this Article 3.4.&#160;&#160;The value of property or services for the 
purpose of this Article 3.4 shall be the value determined by the Directors by 
resolution to be, in all the circumstances of the transaction, no greater than 
the fair market value thereof.&#160;&#160;The full consideration received for a 
share issued by way of dividend shall be the amount determined by the Directors 
to be the amount of the dividend.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">3.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>Subject to the Business
Corporations Act, the Company may issue share purchase warrants, options and 
rights upon such terms and conditions as the Directors determine, which share 
purchase warrants, options and rights may be issued alone or in conjunction with
debentures, debenture stock, bonds, shares or any other securities issued or 
created by the Company from time to time.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 4</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">SHARE REGISTERS</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">4.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The Company shall maintain
at its records office or at another location in British Columbia designated by 
the Directors a central securities register as required by the Business 
Corporations Act.&#160;&#160;The Company may maintain branch securities 
registers at any locations inside or outside British Columbia designated by the 
Directors.&#160;&#160;The Directors may appoint one or more trust companies or 
other persons authorized by the Business Corporations Act (as the case may be, a
&#8220;trust company&#8221;) to maintain the aforesaid central securities 
register and branch securities registers.&#160;&#160;The Directors may also 
appoint one or more trust companies, including the trust company which keeps the
central securities register, as transfer agent for its shares or any class or 
series thereof, as the case may be, and the same or another trust company or 
companies as registrar for its shares or any class or series thereof, as the 
case may be.&#160;&#160;The Directors may terminate the appointment of any such 
trust company at any time and may appoint another trust company in its 
place.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">4.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font>The Company shall not at 
any time close its central securities register.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 5</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TRANSFER OF SHARES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">5.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>A transfer of a share of the Company must not be 
registered unless:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 73px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 49px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="1285">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">a duly signed instrument of transfer in respect of the share 
has been received by the Company;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 73px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="1286">
<div align="justify">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">if a share certificate has been issued by the Company in respect of the 
share to be transferred, that share certificate has been surrendered to the 
Company; and</font></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
</div>
<div align="center">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent"

<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;4 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT:

Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 60px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 60px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="1287">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">if a non-transferable written acknowledgement of the
shareholder&#8217;s right to obtain a share certificate has been issued by the 
Company in respect of the share to be transferred, that acknowledgement has been
surrendered to the Company.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">5.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The instrument of transfer shall be in the 
form, if any, on the back of the Company&#8217;s share certificates or in such 
other form as the Directors may from time to time approve.&#160;&#160;If the 
Directors so require, each instrument of transfer shall be in respect of only 
one class of shares.&#160;&#160;Except to the extent that the Business 
Corporations Act may otherwise provide, the transferor shall be deemed to remain
the holder of the share until the name of the transferee is entered in the 
central securities register or a branch securities register in respect 
thereof.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">5.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The signature of the registered owner of any
shares, or of his duly authorized attorney, upon an authorized instrument of 
transfer shall constitute a complete and sufficient authority to the Company, 
its Directors, officers and agents to register in the name of the transferee as 
named in the instrument of transfer the number of shares specified therein or, 
if no number is specified, all the shares of the registered owner represented by
the share certificates or set out in the written acknowledgments deposited with 
the instrument of transfer.&#160;&#160;If no transferee is named in the 
instrument of transfer, the instrument of transfer shall constitute a complete 
and sufficient authority to the Company, its Directors, officers and agents to 
register, in the name of the person on whose behalf the instrument is deposited 
with the Company for the purpose of having the transfer registered, the number 
of shares specified in the instrument of transfer or, if no number is specified,
all the shares represented by all share certificates or set out in all written 
acknowledgments deposited with the instrument of transfer.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">5.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Company and its Directors, officers and 
agents shall not be bound to enquire into nor as to the title of the person 
named in the form of transfer as transferee or, if no person is named therein as
transferee, of the person on whose behalf the instrument is deposited for the 
purpose of having the transfer registered, or be liable for any claim related to
registering the transfer by the shareholder or by any intermediate owner or 
holder of the shares, or any interest in the shares, or any share certificate 
representing such shares or of any written acknowledgement of a right to obtain 
a share certificate for such shares.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">5.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;There shall be paid to the Company in 
respect of the registration of any transfer such sum, if any, as the Directors 
may from time to time determine.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 6</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TRANSMISSION OF SHARES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">6.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;In the case of the death of a shareholder, 
the survivor or survivors where the deceased was a joint registered holder of 
shares, and the legal personal representative of the deceased shareholder where 
he was the sole holder, shall be the only persons recognized by the Company as 
having any title to his interest in the shares.&#160;&#160;Before recognizing 
any legal personal representative the Directors may require him to produce a 
Court certified copy of a grant of probate or letters of administration, or 
grant of representation, will, order or other instrument or other evidence of 
the death under which title to the shares is claimed to vest, and produce such 
documents and do such things as the Business Corporations Act 
requires.</font><br>
</div>
<div>&#160;
<div>

<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;5 -</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">6.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Upon the death or bankruptcy of a 
shareholder, his personal representative or trustee in bankruptcy, as the case 
may be, although not a shareholder, shall have the same rights, privileges and 
obligations that attach to the shares formerly held by the deceased or bankrupt 
shareholder if the documents and steps required in that regard by the Business 
Corporations Act shall have been deposited with the Company.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">6.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Any person becoming entitled to a share in 
consequence of the death or bankruptcy of a shareholder shall, upon such 
documents and evidence being produced to the Company as the Business 
Corporations Act requires, or who becomes entitled to a share as a result of an 
order of a Court of competent jurisdiction or a statute, have the right either 
to be registered as a shareholder in his representative capacity in respect of 
such share or, if he is a personal representative or trustee in bankruptcy, 
instead of being registered himself, to make such transfer of the share as the 
deceased or bankrupt person could have made.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the 
foregoing, the Directors shall, as regards a transfer by a personal 
representative or trustee in bankruptcy, have the same right, if any, to decline
or suspend registration of a transferee as they would have in the case of a 
transfer of a share by the deceased or bankrupt person before the death or 
bankruptcy.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 7</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">ALTERATION OF AUTHORIZED SHARE STRUCTURE, 
ARTICLES AND NOTICE OF ARTICLES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Subject to Article 7.6 and the provisions of
the Business Corporations Act, the Directors may by resolution change the
authorized share structure of the Company by:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">creating one or more classes or series of shares;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">increasing, reducing or eliminating the maximum number of 
shares that the Company is authorized to issue out of any class or series of 
shares;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">establishing a maximum number of shares that the Company is 
authorized to issue out of any class or series of shares for which no maximum is
established;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 41px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(d)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="836">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">subdividing all or any of the unissued, or fully paid issued, 
shares of the Company with par value into shares of smaller par 
value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 41px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(e)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="836">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">subdividing all or any of the unissued, or fully paid issued, 
shares of the Company without par value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 41px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(f)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="836">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">consolidating all or any of the unissued, or fully paid issued,
shares of the Company with par value into shares of larger par 
value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div>&#160;
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;6 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT:
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(g)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">consolidating all or any of the unissued, or fully paid issued,
shares of the Company without par value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(h)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">if the Company is authorized to issue shares of a class of 
shares with par value:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 91px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 53px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE:
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="781">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">decrease the par value of those shares; or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 92px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 52px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="781">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">increase the par value of those shares if none of the shares of
that class of shares are allotted or issued;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 38px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="839">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">eliminate any class or series of shares of the Company if none 
of the shares of that class or series of shares are allotted or 
issued;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 38px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(j)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="839">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">change all or any of the unissued, or fully paid issued, shares
of the Company with par value into shares without par value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 37px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(k)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="840">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">change all or any of the unissued shares without par value into
shares of the Company with par value;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(l)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="841">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">alter the identifying name of any of the shares of the Company;
and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(m)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="841" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: 
Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">otherwise alter the authorized share structure
of the Company when required or permitted to do so by the Business Corporations 
Act.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Directors may, by resolution, authorize 
and cause the Company to alter its Notice of Articles to reflect any change in 
the authorized share structure of the Company pursuant to Article 7.1 or 
otherwise.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Company may, by ordinary 
resolution:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 37px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="840">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">create special rights or restrictions for, and attach those 
special rights or restrictions to, the shares of any class or series of shares, 
whether or not any or all of those shares have been issued; or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 37px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="840">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">vary or delete any special rights or restrictions attached to 
the shares of any class or series of shares, whether or not any or all of those 
shares have been issued.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Company may, by ordinary resolution, 
alter these Articles to reflect any such creation and attachment, variation or 
deletion of special rights or restrictions pursuant to Article 7.3.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Notwithstanding anything else contained in 
this Part 7, no right or special right attached to issued shares may be 
prejudiced or interfered with unless the shareholders holding shares of the
class or series of shares to which the right or special right is attached 
consent by a separate special resolution of those shareholders.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.6<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Notwithstanding Article 7.1, if any change 
in the authorized share structure of the Company would result in a right or 
special right attached to issued shares being prejudiced or interfered with, 
special rights or restrictions being created and attached to a class or series 
of shares or special rights and restrictions being varied or deleted from a 
class or series of shares, the change must be authorized as provided for in 
Articles 7.4 and 7.5.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div><br>
</div>
<div>
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;7 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.7<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Unless a different type of resolution is 
required by the Business Corporations Act or these Articles, the Directors may
by resolution authorize and cause the Company to make any alterations to its 
Notice of Articles or these Articles.&#160;&#160;Without limiting the generality
of the foregoing, the Directors may by resolution authorize and cause the 
Company to alter its Notice of Articles in order to change its 
name.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">7.8<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Unless these Articles otherwise provide, the
provisions of these Articles relating to shareholder meetings shall apply, with 
the necessary changes and so far as they are applicable, to a class meeting or 
series meeting but the quorum at a class meeting or series meeting shall be one 
person holding or representing by proxy one-third of the shares 
affected.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 8</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PURCHASE OF SHARES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">8.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Subject to the special rights and 
restrictions attached to the shares of any class or series and the Business 
Corporations Act, the Company may, by a resolution of the Directors, purchase or
otherwise acquire any of its shares at the price and upon the terms specified in
such resolution.&#160;&#160;The Company must not make a payment or provide any 
other consideration to purchase or otherwise acquire any of its shares if there 
are reasonable grounds for believing that the Company is insolvent or that 
making the payment or providing the consideration would render the Company 
insolvent.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">8.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;If the Company retains a share redeemed, 
purchased or otherwise acquired by it, the Company may sell, gift or otherwise 
dispose of the share but, while such share is held by the Company, the 
Company:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 39px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="838">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">is not entitled to vote the share at a meeting of its 
shareholders;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 40px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="837">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">must not pay a dividend in respect of the share; 
and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 39px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="838">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">must not make any other distribution in respect of the 
share.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 9</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">BORROWING POWERS</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">9.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Directors may from time to time in their
discretion authorize and cause the Company to:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 39px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="838">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">borrow money in such amount, in such manner, on such security, 
from such sources and upon such terms and conditions as they think 
fit;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 38px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="839">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">guarantee the repayment of money borrowed by any person or the 
performance of any obligation of any person;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 38px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="839">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">issue bonds, debentures, notes and other debt obligations 
either outright or as continuing security for any indebtedness or liability, 
direct or indirect, or obligations of the Company or of any other person; 
and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;
<div>
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;8 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 48px">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 37px">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(d)</font></div>
</td>
<td width="840">
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">mortgage, charge (whether by way of a specific or floating 
charge), grant a security interest in or give other security on the undertaking 
or on the whole or any part of the property and assets of the Company, both 
present and future.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">9.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Any bonds, debentures, notes or other debt 
obligations of the Company may be issued at a discount, premium or otherwise and
with any special privileges as to redemption, surrender, drawing, allotment of 
or conversion into or exchange for shares or other securities, attending and 
voting at meetings of the shareholders of the Company, appointment of Directors 
or otherwise and may by their terms be assignable free from any equities between
the Company and the person to whom they were issued or any subsequent holder 
thereof, all as the Directors may determine.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 10</font></div>
