<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">- 29 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">21.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>Subject to the provisions of the Business Corporations 
Act, the Company may indemnify any person.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">21.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The failure of a Director, alternate Director or officer
of the Company to comply with the provisions of the Business Corporations Act or
these Articles shall not invalidate any indemnity to which he is entitled under 
this Part.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">21.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The Directors may cause the Company to purchase and 
maintain insurance for the benefit of any person (or his heirs or legal personal
representatives) who is or was a Director, officer, alternate Director, employee
or agent of the Company or a person who, at the request of the Company, is or 
was a director, alternate director, officer, employee or agent of another 
corporation, at a time when the corporation is or was an affiliate of the 
Company or a person who, at the request of the Company, is or was or holds or 
held a position equivalent to that of a director, alternate director, officer, 
employee or agent of a partnership, trust, joint venture or other unincorporated
entity and the person&#8217;s heirs or personal representatives against any 
liability incurred by the person as such Director, alternate Director, director,
alternate director, officer, employee, agent or person who holds or held such 
equivalent position.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 22</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIVIDENDS AND RESERVE</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The provisions of this Part 22 are subject to the 
rights, if any, of shareholders holding shares with special rights as to 
dividends.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.2<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>Subject to the Business Corporations Act, the Directors 
may from time to time and at any time declare and authorize payment of such 
dividends on such class or series of shares </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline;
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">of the Company as they may deem 
advisable, to the exclusion of any other class or series of shares.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.3<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The Directors need not give notice to any shareholder of
any declaration under Article 22.2.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.4<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>The Directors may set a date as the record date for the 
purpose of determining shareholders entitled to receive payment of a 
dividend.&#160;&#160;The record date must not precede the date on which the 
dividend is to be paid by more than two months.&#160;&#160;If no record date is 
set, the record date is 5:00 p.m. local time at the place of the registered 
office of the Company on the date on which the Directors pass the resolution 
declaring the dividend.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.5<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>A resolution declaring a dividend may direct payment of 
the dividend wholly or partly by the distribution of specific assets or of fully
paid shares or of bonds, debentures or other securities of the Company, or in 
any one or more of those ways.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.6<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font>If any difficulty arises in regard to a distribution 
under Article 22.5, the Directors may settle the difficulty as they deem 
appropriate, and, in particular, may:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">set the value for distribution of specific assets;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;30 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">determine that cash payments in substitution for all or any 
part of the specific assets to which any shareholders are entitled may be made 
to any shareholders on the basis of the value so fixed in order to adjust the 
rights of all parties; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">vest any such specific assets in trustees for the persons 
entitled to the dividend.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.7<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2"
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-
SPACING: 9pt">&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font></font></font>Any dividend may be made payable on
such date as is fixed by the Directors.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.8<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2"
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;</font></font></font>All dividends on shares of any class or 
series of shares must be declared and paid according to the number of such 
shares held.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.9<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font 
id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-
SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></font></font></font></font></font>If several 
persons are joint shareholders of any share, any one of them may give an 
effective receipt for any dividend, bonus or other money payable in respect of 
the share.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.10<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;No dividend bears interest against the 
Company.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">22.11<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;If a dividend to which a shareholder is 
entitled includes a fraction of the smallest monetary unit of the currency of 
the dividend, that fraction may be disregarded in making payment of the dividend
and that payment represents full payment of the dividend.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">22.12&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Any dividend or other 
distribution payable in cash in respect of shares may be paid by cheque, made 
payable to the order of the person to whom it is sent, and mailed to the address
of the shareholder, or in the case of joint shareholders, to the address of the 
joint shareholder who is first named on the central securities register, or to 
the person and to the address the shareholder or joint shareholders may direct 
in writing.&#160;&#160;The mailing of such cheque </font><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">shall, to the extent of 
the sum represented by the cheque (plus the amount of the tax or other amount
required by law to be deducted), discharge all liability for the dividend unless
such cheque is not paid on presentation or the amount of such tax or other 
amount so deducted is not paid to the appropriate taxing or other 
authority.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">22.13&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding 
anything contained in these Articles, the Directors may from time to time 
capitalize any surplus of the Company and may from time to time issue, as fully 
paid, shares or any bonds, debentures or other securities of the Company as a 
dividend representing the surplus or any part of the surplus.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 23</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DOCUMENTS, RECORDS AND REPORTS</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">23.1<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 
9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;The Directors must cause adequate accounting
records to be kept to record properly the financial affairs and condition of the
Company and to comply with the Business Corporations Act.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">23.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Unless the 
Directors determine otherwise, or unless otherwise determined by ordinary 
resolution, no shareholder of the Company is entitled to inspect or obtain a 
copy of any accounting records of the Company.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">

inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;31 -</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT:

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times
New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 24</font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">NOTICES</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">24.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Unless the 
Business Corporations Act or these Articles provides otherwise, a notice, 
statement, report or other record required or permitted by the Business 
Corporations Act or these Articles to be sent by or to a person may be sent by 
any one of the following methods:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">mail addressed to the person at the applicable address for that
person as follows:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">for a record mailed to a shareholder, the shareholder&#8217;s 
registered address;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">for a record mailed to a Director or officer, the prescribed 
address for mailing shown for the Director or officer in the records kept by the
Company or the mailing address provided by the recipient for the sending of that
record or records of that class; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(iii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">in any other case, the mailing address of the intended 
recipient;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE:

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">delivery at the applicable address for that person as follows, 
addressed to the person:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font

10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">for a record delivered to a shareholder, the 
shareholder&#8217;s registered address;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE:

<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">for a record delivered to a Director or officer, the prescribed
address for delivery shown for the Director or officer in the records kept by 
the Company or the delivery address provided by the recipient for the sending of
that record or records of that class; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(iii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">in any other case, the delivery address of the intended 
recipient;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE:
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">sending the record by fax to the fax number provided by the 
intended recipient for the sending of that record or records of that 
class;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(d)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">sending the record by email to the email address provided by 
the intended recipient for the sending of that record or records of that class; 
or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(e)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">physical delivery to the intended recipient.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">24.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;A record that is 
mailed to a person by ordinary mail to the applicable address for that person 
referred to in Article 24.1 is deemed to be received by the person to whom it 
was mailed on the day, Saturdays, Sundays and holidays excepted, following the 
date of mailing.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">24.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;A certificate 
signed by the Secretary, if any, or other officer of the Company or of any other
corporation acting in that behalf for the Company stating that a notice, 
statement, report or other record was addressed as required by Article 24.1, 
prepaid and mailed or otherwise sent as permitted by Article 24.1 is conclusive 
evidence of that fact.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">- 32 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">24.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;A notice, 
statement, report or other record may be provided by the Company to the joint 
shareholders of a share by providing the notice to the joint shareholder first 
named in the central securities register in respect of the share.</font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">24.5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;A notice, 
statement, report or other record may be provided by the Company to the persons 
entitled to a share in consequence of the death, bankruptcy or incapacity of a 
shareholder by:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">mailing the record, addressed to them:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">by name, by the title of the legal personal representative of 
the deceased or incapacitated shareholder, by the title of trustee of the 
bankrupt shareholder or by any similar description; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">at the address, if any, supplied to the Company for that 
purpose by the persons claiming to be so entitled; or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">if an address referred to in paragraph (a)(ii) has not been 
supplied to the Company, by giving the notice in a manner in which it might have
been given if the death, bankruptcy or incapacity had not occurred.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 25</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">SEAL</font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">25.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Except as provided
in Articles 25.2 and 25.3, the Company&#8217;s seal, if any, must not be 
impressed, affixed or otherwise reproduced on any record except when that 
impression is attested by the signatures of:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">any two Directors;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE:
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">any officer, together with any Director;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">if the Company only has one Director, that Director; 
or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(d)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">any one or more Directors or officers or persons as may be 
determined by the Directors.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">25.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;For the purpose of
certifying under seal a certificate of incumbency of the Directors or officers 
of the Company or a true copy of any resolution or other document, despite 
Article 25.1, the impression of the seal may be attested by the signature of any
Director or officer.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">25.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Directors may 
authorize the seal to be impressed or otherwise reproduced by third parties on 
share certificates or bonds, debentures or other securities of the Company as 
they may determine appropriate from time to time.&#160;&#160;To enable the seal 
to be impressed or otherwise reproduced on any share certificates or bonds, 
debentures or other securities of the Company, whether in definitive or interim 
form, on which facsimiles of any of the signatures of the </font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: 
inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">-&#160;33 -</font></div>
</div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">MacNeill Law 4813</font></font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; 
FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160;</font></div>
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">Directors or officers of the Company are, in accordance with the Business 
Corporations Act<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: 
inline">&#160;</font>or these Articles, printed or otherwise mechanically 
reproduced, there may be delivered to the person employed to engrave, lithograph
or print such definitive or interim share certificates or bonds, debentures or 
other securities one or more unmounted dies or images reproducing the seal and 
the Chair of the Board or any senior officer together with the Secretary, 
Treasurer, Secretary-Treasurer, an Assistant Secretary, an Assistant Treasurer 
or an Assistant Secretary-Treasurer may in writing authorize such person to 
cause the seal to be impressed or otherwise reproduced on such definitive or 
interim share certificates or bonds, debentures or other securities by the use 
of such dies.&#160;&#160;Share certificates or bonds, debentures or other 
securities to which the seal has been so impressed or otherwise reproduced are 
for all purposes deemed to be under and to bear the seal impressed or otherwise 
reproduced on them.</font></div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="HDR">&#160;</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; 
FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PART 26</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 
0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New 
Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">PROHIBITIONS</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">26.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In this Part 
26:</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(a)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;designated security&#8221; means:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">a voting security of the Company;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">a security of the Company that is not a debt security and that 
carries a residual right to participate in the earnings of the Company or, on 
the liquidation or winding up of the Company, in its assets; or</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(iii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">a security of the Company convertible, directly or indirectly, 
into a security described in paragraph (i) or (ii);</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(b)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;security&#8221; has the meaning assigned in the <font 
style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Securities Act</font> (British 
Columbia);</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(c)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;voting security&#8221; means a security of the Company 
that:</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(i)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">is not a debt security; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" 
id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font 
style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">(ii)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 10pt">carries a voting right either under all circumstances or under 
some circumstances that have occurred and are continuing.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">26.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Article 26.3 does 
not apply to the Company if and for so long as it is a public company or a pre-
existing reporting company which has the Statutory Reporting Company Provisions 
as part of its Articles or to which the Statutory Reporting Company Provisions 
apply.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 
0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman;
FONT-SIZE: 
10pt">26.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#16
0;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;No share or 
designated security may be sold, transferred or otherwise disposed of without 
the consent of the Directors and the Directors are not required to give any 
reason for refusing to consent to any such sale, transfer or other 
disposition.</font></div>
